    LONDO= N LETTER LONDON, Wednesday Night. = news of the effect of the
    =E2=80= =A2*- first atom bomb on Hiroshima
    has come thr= ough to-day. No exhilaration has resulted. Let = there no mistake about it. The use = this terrible weapon is generally regarded as justified. But its effects are t= oo terrible to bear prolonged contemplation. O= thers would have used it against us had they be= aten us the race of discovery. None of our enemies has shown us, or the = Chinese, any mercy. The Japanese in espe= cial have been guilty of nearly every form of t= reachery and barbarity. Perhaps they deserve be wiped off the face of the earth, = as those nations were which in= habited the given to the Chosen People" Biblica= l days. Certainly the world will never do much good until the attitude = mind for which the Japanese stand is oblit= erated. And there are 'planes standing by, rea= dy to obliterate them. But the horror that atte= nds the use of this new weapon is very great. not entirely matter of "this might have happened us." There is so= mething deeper, more human, and more decent, behind it. THE BEST <= /span> HOPE "PERHAPS the be= st hope and the =E2=80=A2* best Justification f= or the use of the atom bomb in the Par East are= that may bring the war to a = speedy conclusion without the sacrifice of more valuable British and American lives.= The Japanese, of course, are fanatical. With <= /span> tangible foe every man capable of = bearing arms might well fight until he was killed, and the killing might be long= drawn out and expensive in the lives of our yo= ung men. Whether it will be so when the Japanes= e realise that they cannot combat this <= /a> <= span class=3D"text">new menace, but can only wait until = they are wiped out, or at least their manufactures and their communications, their t= roops and their means of getting these troops t= o the fighting front, is another matter. Already there are signs of a weakening = of spirit in face of this new me= nace. It would not be right to glory too much o= ver it, though some of its manifestations are p= ositively nauseating by reason of their = = hypocrisy.
